        <h3>Fahrassistenz</h3>
        <div class="generated-specs__group-body">
      <div class="spec-row"><span class="spec-row__label">Spurhalteassistent</span><strong class="spec-row__value">Ja (Audi Active Lane Assist), Serienausstattung</strong></div>
